Typographic Subfamily Name NID 17 (MS/BMP/Korean) is missing.
Please verify agains spec. It might be ok if it's a symbol font.

Default

Check gasp table Default.

gasp table default is:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True
and should be:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True
